style="font-size:91%;width:6em;left:6px"><div>OTP</div></div></div></div><div style="padding-top:0.2em">Location within Romania</div></div></div></div></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-header" style="background-color: #DDDDFF; color: black"><a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway"><span style="background-color: #DDDDFF; color:black;">Runways</span></a>\n</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data">\n<table style="width:100%; margin:-2px -1px -1px -1px; border-spacing:0;">\n\n<tbody><tr style="background-color: #e6e6ff">\n<th rowspan="2" style="width: 15%; colspan="2" class="infobox-header" style="background-color: #DDDDFF; color: black"><a href="/wiki/Helipad" title="Helipad"><span style="background-color: #DDDDFF; color:black;">Helipads</span></a>\n</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data">\n<table style="width:100%; margin:-2px -1px -1px -1px; border-spacing:0;">\n\n<tbody><tr style="background-color: #e6e6ff">\n<th rowspan="2" style="width: 15%; border:solid 1px #fafafa; border-width:0 1px 0 0; text-align: center;">Number\n</th>\n<th colspan="2" style="width: 50%; border:solid 1px #fafafa; border-width:0 1px 1px 1px; text-align: center;">Length\n</th>\n<th rowspan="2" style="width: 35%; border:solid 1px #fafafa; border-width:0 0 0 1px; text-align: style="text-align: center;">11\n</td>\n<td style="text-align: center;"><a href="/wiki/Concrete" title="Concrete">Concrete</a>\n</td></tr>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n</tbody></table></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-header" style="background-color: #DDDDFF; color: black">Statistics (2020)</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data"><table class="infobox-subbox"><tbody><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Passengers</th><td class="infobox-data">4,456,577</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Passengers change 2019\xe2\x80\x9320</th><td class="infobox-data"><img alt="Decrease" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Decrease2.svg/11px-Decrease2.svg.png" decoding="async" title="Decrease" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Decrease2.svg/17px-Decrease2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/Decrease2.svg/22px-Decrease2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="300" /> 69.69%</td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label">Aircraft movements</th><td class="infobox-data">52,288</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr style="background-color: #eee"><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data"><div style="text-align: left;">Sources: Romanian <a href="/wiki/Aeronautical_Information_Publication" title="Aeronautical Information Publication">AIP</a> at <a href="/wiki/European_Organisation_for_the_Safety_of_Air_Navigation" class="mw-redirect" title="European Organisation for the Safety of Air Navigation">Eurocontrol</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-AIP_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AIP-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> bucharestairports.ro<sup id="cite_ref-2015buh_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015buh-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Bucharest Henri Coand\xc4\x83 International Airport</b> (<a href="/wiki/Romanian_language" title="Romanian language">Romanian</a>: <i lang="ro">Aeroportul Interna\xc8\x9bional Henri Coand\xc4\x83 Bucure\xc8\x99ti</i>) (<a href="/wiki/IATA_airport_code" title="IATA airport code">IATA</a>: <b>OTP</b>, <a href="/wiki/ICAO_airport_code" title="ICAO airport code">ICAO</a>: <b>LROP</b>) is <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_the_busiest_airports_in_Romania" title="List of the busiest airports in Romania">busiest international airport</a>, located in <a href="/wiki/Otopeni" title="Otopeni">Otopeni</a>, 16.5&#160;km (10.3&#160;mi) north of <a href="/wiki/Bucharest" title="Bucharest">Bucharest</a>\'s city centre.<sup id="cite_ref-AIP_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AIP-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> It is currently one of the three airports serving the capital of Romania. One of them is <a href="/wiki/Aurel_Vlaicu_International_Airport" title="Aurel Vlaicu International Airport">Aurel Vlaicu Airport</a>, which no longer serves scheduled passenger traffic, and the other one <a href="/wiki/Bucharest_Constantin_Br%C3%A2ncu%C8%99i_Airport" title="Bucharest Constantin Br\xc3\xa2ncu\xc8\x99i Airport">Constantin Br\xc3\xa2ncu\xc8\x99i Airport</a>, which is a planned international airport.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The airport is named after Romanian flight pioneer <a href="/wiki/Henri_Coand%C4%83" title="Henri Coand\xc4\x83">Henri Coand\xc4\x83</a>, builder of <a href="/wiki/Coand%C4%83-1910" title="Coand\xc4\x83-1910">Coand\xc4\x83-1910</a> aircraft and discoverer of the <a href="/wiki/Coand%C4%83_effect" title="Coand\xc4\x83 effect">Coand\xc4\x83 effect</a> of <a href="/wiki/Fluidics" title="Fluidics">fluidics</a>. Prior to May 2004, the official name was <i>Bucharest Otopeni International Airport</i> (<a href="/wiki/Romanian_language" title="Romanian language">Romanian</a>: <i>Aeroportul Interna\xc8\x9bional Bucure\xc8\x99ti Otopeni</i>). Henri Coand\xc4\x83 International Airport serves as headquarters for <a href="/wiki/TAROM" title="TAROM">TAROM</a>, the country\'s national airline.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> It also serves as a base of operations for low-cost airlines <a href="/wiki/Animawings" title="Animawings">Animawings</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blue_Air" title="Blue Air">Blue Air</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ryanair" title="Ryanair">Ryanair</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wizz_Air" title="Wizz Air">Wizz Air</a> and charter airlines <a href="/wiki/Air_Bucharest" title="Air Bucharest">Air Bucharest</a> and <a href="/wiki/GullivAir" title="GullivAir">GullivAir</a>. It is managed by The National Company Bucharest Airports S.A. (<i>Compania Na\xc8\x9bional\xc4\x83 Aeroporturi Bucure\xc8\x99ti S.A.</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> The military section of the airport is used by the <a href="/wiki/RoAF_90th_Airlift_Base" title="RoAF 90th Airlift Base">90th Airlift Flotilla</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Romanian_Air_Force" title="Romanian Air Force">Romanian Air Force</a>.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#History"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span class="toctext">History</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li routes</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-12"><a href="#Ground_transportation"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Ground tocsection-14"><a href="#Bus"><span class="tocnumber">6.2</span> <span class="toctext">Bus</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15"><a href="#Car"><span class="tocnumber">6.3</span> <span class="toctext">Car</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-16"><a href="#Taxi"><span class="tocnumber">6.4</span> <span class="toctext">Taxi</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-17"><a href="#Incidents_and_accidents"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">Incidents and accidents</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 class="tocnumber">9</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-20"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">10</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_years">Early years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg/220px-CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="139" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg/330px-CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg/440px-CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg 2x" data-file-width="447" data-file-height="283" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CezarLazarescu-OTP-1970.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Architect <a href="/wiki/Cezar_L%C4%83z%C4%83rescu" title="Cezar L\xc4\x83z\xc4\x83rescu">Cezar L\xc4\x83z\xc4\x83rescu</a></div></div></div>\n<p>During <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the airport in Otopeni was used as an airbase by the <a href="/wiki/Luftwaffe" title="Luftwaffe">German Air Force</a>. Until 1965, it was a major airfield for the <a href="/wiki/Romanian_Air_Force" title="Romanian Air Force">Romanian Air Force</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Aurel_Vlaicu_International_Airport" title="Aurel Vlaicu International Airport">B\xc4\x83neasa Airport</a> serving as Bucharest\'s commercial airport. In 1965, with the growth of air traffic, the Otopeni airbase was converted to a commercial airport. The runway was modernized and extended to 3,500 metres (11,500&#160;ft) from the previous 1,200 metres (3,900&#160;ft), making it one of the longest in Europe at that time.<sup id="cite_ref-2007Report_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007Report-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In August 1969, when <a href="/wiki/United_States_President" class="mw-redirect" title="United States President">United States President</a> <a href="/wiki/Richard_Nixon" title="Richard Nixon">Nixon</a> visited Romania, a VIP lounge was inaugurated. A new passenger terminal (designed by <a href="/wiki/Cezar_L%C4%83z%C4%83rescu" title="Cezar L\xc4\x83z\xc4\x83rescu">Cezar L\xc4\x83z\xc4\x83rescu</a>), with a capacity of 1,200,000 passengers per year, was opened on 13 April 1970, for domestic and international flights.<sup id="cite_ref-2007Report_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007Report-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> An improvement program added a second runway in 1986, expanding capacity to 35 aircraft movements per hour.<sup id="cite_ref-2007Report_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007Report-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 1992, Otopeni Airport became a regular member of <a href="/wiki/Airports_Council_International" title="Airports Council International">Airports Council International</a> (ACI).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Expansion_since_the_1990s">Expansion since the 1990s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Expansion since the 1990s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The first stage of the plan (Phase I), taking place between 1994 and 1998, involved the construction of a new departures terminal and of a new <a href="/wiki/Airside_(airport)" class="mw-redirect" title="Airside (airport)">airside</a> <a href="/wiki/Concourse" title="Concourse">concourse</a> with five <a href="/wiki/Jetways" class="mw-redirect" title="Jetways">jetways</a> and nine gates (referred to as \'the Finger\') as well as the extension of <a href="/wiki/Airport_ramp" class="mw-redirect" title="Airport ramp">airport ramps</a> and of their associated <a href="/wiki/Taxiway" title="Taxiway">taxiways</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-mt.ro_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mt.ro-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The second phase (labeled Phase II/IIe) of the plan led to the construction of a terminal dedicated to domestic flights and of a multi-story car park (2003), the complete overhaul of the <a href="/wiki/Control_tower" class="mw-redirect" title="Control tower">control tower</a> (between 2005\xe2\x80\x932007) as well as the transformation of the old terminal building in a dedicated arrivals hall (in 2000). During the same phase, two high-speed taxiways (Victor and Whiskey) were constructed. Phase II was completed in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-mt.ro_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mt.ro-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The third stage of the plan (Phase III), which started in 2009, involved the extension of the airside concourse (\'the Finger\') with 15 new gates (nine of which have jetways), as well as the expansion of the Departure Hall (with 8 new gates). The airside concourse extension, designed by Studio Capelli Architettura &amp; Associati, and measuring 17,000 square metres (200,000&#160;sq&#160;ft), was inaugurated on 29 March 2011.<sup id="cite_ref-mt.ro_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mt.ro-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-a10_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-a10-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> It was followed, in November 2012, by the extension of the Departure Hall to a total area of 38,600 square metres (400,000&#160;sq&#160;ft).<sup id="cite_ref-Departure_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Departure-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-avimag_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-avimag-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In March 2012, all air traffic except for business air traffic was transferred from <a href="/wiki/Aurel_Vlaicu_International_Airport" title="Aurel Vlaicu International Airport">Aurel Vlaicu International Airport</a> (at that time Bucharest\'s low-cost hub) to Henri Coand\xc4\x83 International Airport.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Terminals">Terminals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Terminals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The airport\'s facilities consist of a single <a href="/wiki/Airport_terminal" title="Airport terminal">terminal</a> with three main facilities (colloquially referred to as "Terminals"): the Departures Hall/Terminal, the Arrivals Hall/Terminal, and the Finger Terminal (the airside concourse).<sup id="cite_ref-Schengen_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Schengen-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> A walkway with shops connects the departures and arrivals buildings. The airside concourse is organized in two (domestic and international) passengers flows.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> The entire terminal has 104 check-in desks, 38 gates (of which 14 are equipped with <a href="/wiki/Jet_bridge" title="Jet bridge">jetways</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-Departure_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Departure-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and a total floor area of 86,000 square metres (930,000&#160;sq&#160;ft).<sup id="cite_ref-2007Report_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2007Report-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-a10_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-a10-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-avimag_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-avimag-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Future_development">Future development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Future development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Beyond Phase III, a new terminal building (Henri Coand\xc4\x83 2) at the eastern end of the current location is envisaged. Henri Coand\xc4\x83 2 will be of a modular design, consisting of four separate buildings, each capable of handling 5 million passengers annually. Each module will be built as traffic demands dictate. By 2030, Terminal 2 alone should be able to handle the expected volume of 20 million passengers per year. The terminal will be directly connected to the <a href="/wiki/A3_motorway_(Romania)" title="A3 motorway (Romania)">A3 motorway</a> and to the <a href="/wiki/C%C4%83ile_Ferate_Rom%C3%A2ne" title="C\xc4\x83ile Ferate Rom\xc3\xa2ne">railway system</a>. However, the plans might get delayed due to funding problems. There is a chance however that, if funds can be allocated in time, the airport can open its new terminal by 2025.\n</p><p>On 18 January 2021, it has been announced that the airport purchased all the land it needs in order to begin the expansion.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> However, due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, work is set to begin in 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Airlines_and_destinations">Airlines and destinations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Airlines and destinations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Passenger">Passenger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Passenger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="font-size:95%"><tbody><tr><th>Airlines</th><th class="unsortable">Destinations</th></tr><tr><td><a href="#cite_note-Anna.aero_database-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, the airport handled 13.8 million passengers (63.3% of the total number of passengers carried by Romanian airports) and 39,534 tons of cargo (81.4% of the total amount of cargo handled by Romanian airports).<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><br />\n</p>\n<style href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> INSSE<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup></i></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ground_transportation">Ground transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Ground transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rail">Rail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Rail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>An <a href="/wiki/Airport_rail_link" title="Airport rail link">airport rail link</a> service to the main railway station, <a href="/wiki/Gara_de_Nord" class="mw-redirect" title="Gara de Nord">Gara de Nord</a> (Bucharest North), runs from the Airport railway station located near the parking lot of the Arrivals hall.<sup id="cite_ref-train_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-train-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> As of December 2020, the trains, alternately operated by <a href="/wiki/C%C4%83ile_Ferate_Rom%C3%A2ne" title="C\xc4\x83ile Ferate Rom\xc3\xa2ne">CFR</a>, <a href="/wiki/Regio_C%C4%83l%C4%83tori" title="Regio C\xc4\x83l\xc4\x83tori">Regio</a> and <a href="/wiki/Transferoviar_C%C4%83l%C4%83tori" title="Transferoviar C\xc4\x83l\xc4\x83tori">TFC</a>, travels in 20 minutes, departing every 40 minutes, seven days a week.<sup id="cite_ref-train_82-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-train-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>\nA new <a href="/wiki/Bucharest_Metro_Line_M6" title="Bucharest Metro Line M6">Metro Line M6</a> is also planned, connecting the airport to the Gara de Nord train station, and integrating the airport into the <a href="/wiki/Bucharest_Metro" title="Bucharest Metro">Bucharest Metro</a> network.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png/200px-Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png" decoding="async" width="200" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png/300px-Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d1/Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png/400px-Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png 2x" data-file-width="1449" data-file-height="1031" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bucharest_Airport_Bus_783_route.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>RATB Route 783 diagram (connections to <a href="/wiki/Bucharest_Metro" title="Bucharest Metro">Bucharest Metro</a> lines shown)</div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bus">Bus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Bus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Henri Coand\xc4\x83 Airport is connected to the public transport company <a href="/wiki/Societatea_de_Transport_Bucure%C8%99ti" title="Societatea de Transport Bucure\xc8\x99ti">STB</a> system. The 780 route provides express bus service to <a href="/wiki/Gara_de_Nord" class="mw-redirect" title="Gara de Nord">Gara de Nord</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gara_Basarab" class="mw-redirect" title="Gara Basarab">Gara Basarab</a> railway stations in Bucharest and the routes 783 and 784 provide express bus service to the city center (<a href="/wiki/Pia%C8%9Ba_Unirii" title="Pia\xc8\x9ba Unirii">Pia\xc8\x9ba Unirii</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> Route 783 to the city center is running 24 hours a day.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Car">Car</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Car">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The airport is 16.5&#160;km (10.3&#160;mi) north of central <a href="/wiki/Bucharest" title="Bucharest">Bucharest</a>, to which it is connected by route <a href="/wiki/DN1" title="DN1">DN1</a>. The <a href="/wiki/A3_motorway_(Romania)" title="A3 motorway (Romania)">A3 motorway</a> will connect the future terminal 2 and the city.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Taxi">Taxi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Taxi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>As of May 2013, taxis serving Henri Coand\xc4\x83 Airport can be ordered using a touch screen system in the arrivals terminal, allowing the taxi drivers to enter the pick-up area. This measure was taken after many complaints from passengers who were being ripped off when using illegal, high-price taxis.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">Uber</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bolt_(company)" title="Bolt (company)">Bolt</a> are also available at the airport.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Incidents_and_accidents">Incidents and accidents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Henri_Coand%C4%83_International_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Incidents and accidents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li>On 31 March 1995, <a href="/wiki/TAROM_Flight_371" title="TAROM Flight 371">TAROM Flight 371</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Airbus_A310" title="Airbus A310">Airbus A310-324</a> registered as YR-LCC, simultaneously experienced asymmetric thrust during climb and one of the pilots being incapacitated. The plane crashed near <a href="/wiki/Balote%C5%9Fti" class="mw-redirect" title="Balote\xc5\x9fti">Balote\xc5\x9fti</a> just two minutes after takeoff. All 60 people aboard were killed.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>On 30 December 2007, a TAROM <a href="/wiki/Boeing_737" title="Boeing 737">Boeing 737-300</a> (YR-BGC "Constan\xc8\x9ba"), flying <a href="/wiki/TAROM_Flight_3107" title="TAROM Flight 3107">Flight 3107</a> hit a car on the runway while taking off for <a href="/wiki/Sharm-el-Sheikh" class="mw-redirect" title="Sharm-el-Sheikh">Sharm-el-Sheikh</a>. The aircraft stopped beside the runway and was severely damaged.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a Europe by passenger traffic">List of the busiest airports in Europe by passenger traffic</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_the_busiest_airports_in_Romania" title="List of the busiest airports in
